  leaving the GitHub Actions workflow as the canonical deployment
  path.

## Current phase

- Phase 2 through Phase 6 are complete; Phase 7 coverage refinement is active.
- Phase 8 is now defined as the next breadth-expansion
  stage: add new patterns, newly justified domains, and
  their linked grounded instances only after Phase 7 closes
  the highest-leverage refinement pressure inside the current
  matrix.
- Canonical pattern coverage spans all nine pattern families, all tracked architecture types, and the full `low` / `moderate` / `high` / `critical` risk ladder.
- Grounded coverage now spans three hundred seventy-one examples across all seven modeled domains, with `compliance` at fifty-five grounded examples, `finance` at fifty-four, `operations`, `research`, plus `hr` at fifty-three, and `engineering` plus `support` at fifty-two. Phase 7 should still optimize for structurally thin pattern slices rather than simple domain-count balancing while avoiding immediate reuse of the just-refreshed HR threshold-calibration lane and the broader set of recently touched approval, recommendation, investigation, and live-execution surfaces captured in the checkpoint list below.
- All canonical patterns remain grounded at least once at the instance layer; after deepening `adaptive-threshold-calibration` in `hr` with a governed work-authorization expiry threshold example, the current highest-leverage move is to rebalance either `engineering` or `support` through a materially distinct bounded slice so Phase 7 keeps broadening depth without reopening canonical metadata.
- Browse artifacts remain derived from canonical pattern truth and should only change when a new grounding exposes genuine drift.
- The validation and publication baseline remains `uv run python scripts/python/validate_yaml.py`, `uv run python scripts/python/build_site_docs.py`, and `uv run mkdocs build`.

## Ordered tasks

1. Continue Phase 7 with one instance-only refinement in another materially distinct slice outside the just-refreshed `adaptive-threshold-calibration` HR lane, the recent research digest and crisis-briefing lanes, and the broader set of refreshed approval, recommendation, investigation, and live-execution surfaces. The current working candidate should come from one of the remaining 52-instance domains (`engineering` or `support`) and stay centered on one exact governed artifact rather than another immediate low-risk optimization repeat.
2. Keep the result bounded at one exact governed artifact with explicit source precedence, prerequisite frozen state, visible blockers, revision-aware or append-only lineage, and named owner accountability.
3.
